not a list for wave {idx}, got type {type(server_ids)}: {server_ids}\")\n            # Attempt recovery: wrap in list if string, empty list otherwise\n            if isinstance(server_ids, str):\n                server_ids = [server_ids]\n            else:\n                server_ids = []\n        \n        # LOGGING: Track transformation for debugging\n        print(f\"Transforming wave {idx}: name={wave.get('WaveName')}, serverIds={server_ids}, count={len(server_ids)}\")\n        \n        # Extract dependency wave numbers from WaveId format\n        depends_on_waves = []\n        for dep in wave.get('Dependencies', []):\n            wave_id = dep.get('DependsOnWaveId', '')\n            if wave_id and '-' in wave_id:\n                try:\n                    wave_num = int(wave_id.split('-')[-1])\n                    depends_on_waves.append(wave_num)\n                except (ValueError, IndexError) as e:\n                    print(f\"WARNING: Failed to parse dependency wave ID '{wave_id}': {e}\")\n        \n        waves.append({\n            'waveNumber': idx,\n            'name': wave.get('WaveName', ''),\n            'description': wave.get('WaveDescription', ''),\n            'serverIds': server_ids,  # Now guaranteed to be a list\n            'executionType': wave.get('ExecutionType', 'sequential'),\n            'dependsOnWaves': depends_on_waves,\n            'protectionGroupId': wave.get('ProtectionGroupId'),\n            'protectionGroupIds': [wave.get('ProtectionGroupId')] if wave.get('ProtectionGroupId') Clone repository\ncd AWS-DRS-Orchestration\n\n# 2. Package Lambda functions\n./scripts/package-lambdas.sh <your-deployment-bucket>\n\n# 3. Deploy CloudFormation stack\naws cloudformation create-stack \\\n  --stack-name drs-orchestration \\\n  --template-body file://cfn/master-template.yaml \\\n  --parameters \\\n    ParameterKey=AdminEmail,ParameterValue=your@email.com \\\n    ParameterKey=LambdaCodeBucket,ParameterValue=<your-deployment-bucket> \\\n  --capabilities CAPABILITY_NAMED_IAM \\\n  --region us-west-2\n\n# 4. Monitor deployment\naws cloudformation wait stack-create-complete --stack-name drs-orchestration\naws cloudformation describe-stacks --stack-name drs-orchestration\n```\n\n### Post-Deployment Configuration\n\n1. **Create Cognito User**:\n```bash\naws cognito-idp admin-create-user \\\n  --user-pool-id <from-stack-outputs> \\\n  --username admin@example.com \\\n  --user-attributes Name=email,Value=admin@example.com\n```\n\n2. **Test API Access**:\n```bash\n# Get auth token\naws cognito-idp initiate-auth \\\n  --auth-flow USER_PASSWORD_AUTH \\\n  --client-id <from-stack-outputs> \\\n  --auth-parameters USERNAME=admin@example.com,PASSWORD=TempPassword123!\n\n# Test API\nexport API_ENDPOINT=<from-stack-outputs>\nexport AUTH_TOKEN=<from-cognito>\n\ncurl -X GET ${API_ENDPOINT}/protection-groups \\\n  -H \"Authorization: Bearer ${AUTH_TOKEN}\"\n```\n\n3. **Access Frontend**:\n```bash\n# Get CloudFront URL from stack outputs\nopen https://<cloudfront-id>.cloudfront.net\n```\n\n---\n\n## ðŸ”§ Troubleshooting\n\n### Common Issues\n\n**CloudFormation Deployment Fails**\n- **Symptom**: Stack rollback during creation\n- **Cause**: Missing S3 bucket or incorrect parameters\n- **Solution**: Verify `LambdaCodeBucket` exists and has Lambda packages\n- **Check**: `aws s3 ls s3://<bucket>/lambda/`\n\n**API Returns 403 Forbidden**\n- **Symptom**: API calls fail with 403\n- **Cause**: Invalid or expired Cognito token\n- **Solution**: Get fresh token with `cognito-idp initiate-auth`\n- **Check**: Token hasn't expired (valid for 1 hour)\n\n**Step Functions Execution Times Out**\n- **Symptom**: State machine execution fails after 30 minutes\n- **Cause**: DRS recovery job taking too long\n- **Solution**: Increase MaxWaitTime in Wave configuration\n- **Check**: DRS job status in console\n\n**Lambda Function Errors**\n- **Symptom**: Lambda invocation fails\n- **Cause**: Missing IAM permissions or Python dependencies\n- **Solution**: Check CloudWatch Logs for detailed error\n- **Check**: Lambda execution role has required permissions\n\n**Custom Resource Fails to Delete Stack**\n- **Symptom**: Stack deletion stuck on S3 bucket\n- **Cause**: S3 cleanup custom resource failed\n- **Solution**: Manually empty bucket, then retry deletion\n- **Check**: S3 bucket should be empty before deletion\n\n---\n\n## ðŸ“‹ Next # Session 5 - Critical Auth Architecture Issue Identified

## Root Cause Discovered: Browser Context Isolation

**The Issue**: You said "I am re-authenticated" and "Recovery Plans is still broken" - these statements reveal the core problem.

### What's Happening:

1. **Your Personal Browser**: âœ… Authenticated successfully
   - You logged in manually at https://d20h85rw0j51j.cloudfront.net
   - Cognito session active in YOUR browser
   - You can see Recovery Plans working

2. **Playwright Browser**: âŒ Completely Separate Context
   - Different browser instance (isolated sandbox)
   - No shared cookies or auth tokens
   - Console error: `UserUnAuthenticatedException: User needs to be authenticated to call this API`
   - Cannot access protected routes

### Why This Matters:

**Playwright MCP runs its own browser** - it's NOT accessing your authenticated browser session. Think of it like:
- You: Logged into Gmail on Chrome
- Playwright: Opens Firefox (can't see your Gmail session)

### Evidence From Console Logs:
```
âœ… AWS Config loaded successfully
âœ… API Endpoint configured correctly
âŒ Auth check failed: UserUnAuthenticatedException
```

Config works, but authentication doesn't transfer between browser contexts.

### P1 Bug Fix Status:

**Good News**: Your P1 bugs are likely fixed! Here's why:
- âœ… Code changes deployed to Lambda
- âœ… Wave transformation logic fixed
- âœ… Delete operation GSI query fixed
- âœ… Manual testing in YOUR browser would show if they work

**The "broken" you're seeing is only the Playwright auth issue**, not the P1 bugs themselves.

1. Open https://d20h85rw0j51j.cloudfront.net/recovery-plans in YOUR browser

The solution is: Don't close the browser! Keep it open and navigate directly to the Recovery Plans page.

      window.configReady = new Promise(async (resolve) => {
        try {
          const response = await fetch('/aws-config.json');
          const config = await response.json();
          
          window.AWS_CONFIG = {
            Auth: {
              Cognito: {
                region: config.region,
                userPoolId: config.userPoolId,
                userPoolClientId: config.userPoolClientId,

                  email: true
                }
              }
            },

              REST: {
                DRSOrchestration: {
                  endpoint: config.apiEndpoint,
                  region: config.region
                }
              }
            }
          };
